<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кондуктор.html>кондуктор</a> (14604)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кондуктор.html>конду́ктор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kondúktor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кондуктор.html>конду́ктора</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кондуктор.html>кондуктора́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кондуктор.html>конду́кторы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кондуктор.html>кондукторо́в</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кондуктор.html>конду́кторов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>conductor</li>
<li>railroad conductor, guard</li></ol>

***конек.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:конек.html>конёк</a> (7066)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конь.html>конь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">konʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ёк</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конек.html>конёк</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">konjók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конек.html>конька́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конек.html>коньки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конек.html>конько́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конь.html>конь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">konʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: (little) horse, horsy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морской.html>морско́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:конек.html>конёк</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">morskój <b>konjók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">seahorse</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:конек.html>Конёк</a></b>-горбуно́к</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Konjók</b>-Gorbunók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Konyok-Gorbunok ("Little Humpbacked Horse" in the Slavic mythology)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> skate (ice skate or roller skate)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">одноря́дный ро́ликовый <b><a href = vnd.unilang:конек.html>конёк</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">odnorjádnyj rólikovyj <b>konjók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in-line skate</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hobby, fad, soapbox, favourite subject
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сесть.html>сесть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своего́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:конек.html>конька́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sestʹ na svojevó <b>konʹká</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pursue one's favorite subject, to mount one's hobby-horse</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pipit (bird)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(roof)</i> ridge, finial</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:конец.html>конец</a> (144)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">коньць</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">konĭcĭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">end; edge, border</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*konьcь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">end</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*konъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">beginning; end</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ьcь</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čęti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to begin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конец.html>коне́ц</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">konéc</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конец.html>конца́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конец.html>концы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конец.html>концо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>end</li>
<li>ending, close, termination</li>
<li>death</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">familiar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> distance, way</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> male sex organ</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rope</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> borough <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in medieval Novgorod</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***конечность.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:конечность.html>коне́чность</a> (5036)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конечный.html>коне́чный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">konéčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

***конкретизировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:конкретизировать.html>конкретизи́ровать</a> (28819)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">konkretisieren</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конкретизировать.html>конкретизи́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">konkretizírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to concretize</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***конкурент.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:конкурент.html>конкуре́нт</a> (6269)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конкурент.html>конкуре́нт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">konkurént</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конкурент.html>конкуре́нта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конкурент.html>конкуре́нты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конкурент.html>конкуре́нтов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>competitor, rival (person against whom one is competing)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>Judging by the stress borrowed via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">konkurs</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">concursus</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:конница.html>ко́нница</a> (16515)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*konьnica</i>, equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конный.html>ко́нный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">konnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ица</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конница.html>ко́нница</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kónnica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конница.html>ко́нницы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конница.html>ко́нницы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конница.html>ко́нниц</a></b>)

***конный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:конный.html>ко́нный</a> (24814)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*konьnъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конный.html>ко́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> horse
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конный.html>ко́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двор.html>двор</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kónnyj dvor</i> ― <span class="e-translation">stables</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конный.html>ко́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:завод.html>заво́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kónnyj zavód</i> ― <span class="e-translation">stud farm</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:конный.html>ко́нная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:статуя.html>ста́туя</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kónnaja</b> státuja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">equestrian statue</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:конный.html>ко́нный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:спорт.html>спорт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kónnyj</b> sport</i> ― <span class="e-translation">equestrian sport</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cavalry; mounted
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конный.html>ко́нная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:армия.html>а́рмия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kónnaja ármija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Cavalry</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>horse-drawn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:конный.html>ко́нный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:привод.html>привод</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kónnyj</b> privod</i> ― <span class="e-translation">horse drive</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:конный.html>ко́нная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тяга.html>тя́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kónnaja</b> tjága</i> ― <span class="e-translation">horse traction</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конь.html>конь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">konʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кони́на</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">konína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***конопля.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:конопля.html>конопля́</a> (23791)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Dialectally vocalized also <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конопля.html>коно́пля</a></span>, which is probably the original stress of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*konopľa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hemp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конопля.html>конопля́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">konopljá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конопля.html>конопли́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конопля.html>конопли́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конопля.html>конопле́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cannabis, hemp</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">коноплянка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">konopljanka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">конопляный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">konopljanyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:консервативный.html>консервати́вный</a> (11350)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">konservativ</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:консервативный.html>консервати́вный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">konservatívnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)консервати́внее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)консервати́вней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>conservative
<dl><dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonyms:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радикальный.html>радика́льный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">radikálʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:революционный.html>революцио́нный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">revoljuciónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> nonsurgical
<dl><dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хирургический.html>хирурги́ческий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">xirurgíčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:консервный.html>консе́рвный</a> (8153)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:консервы.html>консе́рвы</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">konsérvy</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:консервный.html>консе́рвный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">konsérvnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tinned food, canned food
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:консервный.html>консе́рвная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:фабрика.html>фа́брика</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>konsérvnaja</b> fábrika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tinned food factory; cannery</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:консервный.html>консе́рвная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:промышленность.html>промы́шленность</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>konsérvnaja</b> promýšlennostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">preserved/tinned food industry; canning industry</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:консервный.html>консе́рвная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:банк.html>ба́нка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">konsérvnaja bánka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tin; can; jar</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:консервный.html>консе́рвный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нож.html>но́ж</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">konsérvnyj nóž</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tin opener; can opener</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***консилиум.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:консилиум.html>конси́лиум</a> (23286)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cōnsilium</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:консилиум.html>конси́лиум</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">konsílium</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:консилиум.html>конси́лиума</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:консилиум.html>конси́лиумы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:консилиум.html>конси́лиумов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> meeting or consultation among several doctors</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> conference of professionals</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:конский.html>ко́нский</a> (10236)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конь.html>конь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">konʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конский.html>ко́нский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kónskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> horse
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:конский.html>ко́нский</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лос</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kónskij</b> vólos</i> ― <span class="e-translation">horsehair</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:конский.html>ко́нская</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:амуниция.html>амуни́ция</a>; <b><a href = vnd.unilang:конский.html>ко́нское</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:снаряжение.html>снаряже́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kónskaja</b> amunícija; <b>kónskoje</b> snarjažénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">harness</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:конский.html>ко́нское</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поголовье.html>поголо́вье</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kónskoje</b> pogolóvʹje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">number of horses; <b>horse</b> population</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:конский.html>ко́нская</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:щетка.html>щётка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kónskaja</b> ščótka</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>horse</b> brush</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:конский.html>ко́нский</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:щавель.html>щаве́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kónskij</b> ščavélʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">horse sorrel; monk's rhubarb</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***конспиративный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:конспиративный.html>конспирати́вный</a> (20636)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">konspirativ</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конспиративный.html>конспирати́вный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">konspiratívnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)конспирати́внее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)конспирати́вней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>conspiratorial, secret, underground, clandestine</li></ol>
